Hie\xcc\xa3\xcc\x82n \xc4\x91ang \xc4\x91u\xcc\x9bo\xcc\x9b\xcc\xa3c ca\xcc\x81ch ly, \xc4\x91ie\xcc\x82\xcc\x80u tri\xcc\xa3 ta\xcc\xa3i Trung ta\xcc\x82m Y te\xcc\x82\xcc\x81 Tha\xcc\x80nh pho\xcc\x82\xcc\x81 Ha\xcc\x80 Tie\xcc\x82n, ti\xcc\x89nh Kie\xcc\x82n Giang.</p>\n\n<p>b. 75 ca ghi nha\xcc\xa3\xcc\x82n trong nu\xcc\x9bo\xcc\x9b\xcc\x81c</p>\n\n<p>- CA BE\xcc\xa3\xcc\x82NH BN9029-BNBN9033, BN9037, BN9039-BN9040, BN9042, BN9044-BN9045, BN9048-BN9053, BN9055-BN9067, BN9069-BN9093 ghi nha\xcc\xa3\xcc\x82n ta\xcc\xa3i ti\xcc\x89nh Ba\xcc\x86\xcc\x81c Giang trong khu ca\xcc\x81ch ly va\xcc\x80 khu vu\xcc\x9b\xcc\xa3c \xc4\x91a\xcc\x83 \xc4\x91u\xcc\x9bo\xcc\x9b\xcc\xa3c phong to\xcc\x89a, lie\xcc\x82n quan \xc4\x91e\xcc\x82\xcc\x81n co\xcc\x82ng nha\xcc\x82n la\xcc\x80m ta\xcc\xa3i ca\xcc\x81c khu co\xcc\x82ng nghie\xcc\xa3\xcc\x82p. Ke\xcc\x82\xcc\x81t qua\xcc\x89 xe\xcc\x81t nghie\xcc\xa3\xcc\x82m du\xcc\x9bo\xcc\x9bng ti\xcc\x81nh vo\xcc\x9b\xcc\x81i SARS-CoV-2.</p>\n\n<p>- CA BE\xcc\xa3\xcc\x82NH BN9034-BN9036, BN9038 ghi nha\xcc\xa3\xcc\x82n ta\xcc\xa3i ti\xcc\x89nh Ba\xcc\x86\xcc\x81c Ninh: 2 ca lie\xcc\x82n quan \xc4\x91e\xcc\x82\xcc\x81n o\xcc\x82\xcc\x89 di\xcc\xa3ch Khu co\xcc\x82ng nghie\xcc\xa3\xcc\x82p Que\xcc\x82\xcc\x81 Vo\xcc\x83, 2 ca lie\xcc\x82n quan \xc4\x91e\xcc\x82\xcc\x81n o\xcc\x82\xcc\x89 di\xcc\xa3ch Khu co\xcc\x82ng nghie\xcc\xa3\xcc\x82p Kha\xcc\x86\xcc\x81c Nie\xcc\xa3\xcc\x82m. Ke\xcc\x82\xcc\x81t qua\xcc\x89 xe\xcc\x81t nghie\xcc\xa3\xcc\x82m du\xcc\x9bo\xcc\x9bng ti\xcc\x81nh vo\xcc\x9b\xcc\x81i SARS-CoV-2.</p>\n\n<p>- CA BE\xcc\xa3\xcc\x82NH BN9068 ghi nha\xcc\xa3\xcc\x82n ta\xcc\xa3i Be\xcc\xa3\xcc\x82nh vie\xcc\xa3\xcc\x82n Be\xcc\xa3\xcc\x82nh Nhie\xcc\xa3\xcc\x82t \xc4\x91o\xcc\x9b\xcc\x81i Trung u\xcc\x9bo\xcc\x9bng co\xcc\x9b so\xcc\x9b\xcc\x89 \xc4\x90o\xcc\x82ng Anh (la\xcc\x80 nha\xcc\x82n vie\xcc\x82n y te\xcc\x82\xcc\x81 thu\xcc\x9b\xcc\xa3c hie\xcc\xa3\xcc\x82n nhie\xcc\xa3\xcc\x82m vu\xcc\xa3 cha\xcc\x86m so\xcc\x81c \xc4\x91ie\xcc\x82\xcc\x80u tri\xcc\xa3 b\xe1\xbb\x87nh nh\xc3\xa2n COVID-19).</p>\n\n<p>- CA BE\xcc\xa3\xcc\x82NH BN9041, BN9043, BN9046-BN9047, BN9054 ghi nha\xcc\xa3\xcc\x82n ta\xcc\xa3i ti\xcc\x89nh La\xcc\xa3ng So\xcc\x9bn: la\xcc\x80 F1 cu\xcc\x89a BN8794, \xc4\x91a\xcc\x83 \xc4\x91u\xcc\x9bo\xcc\x9b\xcc\xa3c ca\xcc\x81ch ly. Ke\xcc\x82\xcc\x81t qua\xcc\x89 xe\xcc\x81t nghie\xcc\xa3\xcc\x82m nga\xcc\x80y 07/6/2021 du\xcc\x9bo\xcc\x9bng ti\xcc\x81nh vo\xcc\x9b\xcc\x81i SARS-CoV-2. Hie\xcc\xa3\xcc\x82n \xc4\x91ang \xc4\x91u\xcc\x9bo\xcc\x9b\xcc\xa3c ca\xcc\x81ch ly, \xc4\x91ie\xcc\x82\xcc\x80u tri\xcc\xa3 ta\xcc\xa3i Trung ta\xcc\x82m Y te\xcc\x82\xcc\x81 huye\xcc\xa3\xcc\x82n Hu\xcc\x9b\xcc\x83u Lu\xcc\x83ng, ti\xcc\x89nh La\xcc\xa3ng So\xcc\x9bn.</p>\n\n<p>- CA BE\xcc\xa3\xcc\x82NH BN9094-BN9103 ghi nha\xcc\xa3\xcc\x82n ta\xcc\xa3i TP.
